+"""Test workarounds for bf16 tl.dot bug on SM120."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I = 128, 4096, 1536
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w_gate = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_up = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+
+# Full reference
+gate_ref = x @ w_gate
+up_ref = x @ w_up
+out_ref = torch.nn.functional.silu(gate_ref) * up_ref
+
+BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N, BLOCK_K = 64, 128, 32
+num_nt = triton.cdiv(I, BLOCK_N)
+
+@triton.jit
+def full_kernel(
+    x_ptr, wg_ptr, wu_ptr, out_ptr,
+    n_tokens, H, I,
+    x_s0, wg_s0, wu_s0, out_s0,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+    USE_FP16: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    n_start = nt * BLOCK_N
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+
+            a_raw = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < n_tokens,
+            )
+            wg_raw = tl.load(
+                wg_ptr + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wg_s0 + (n_start + n_off)[None, :],
+                mask=(k_base + k_off)[:, None] < H,
+            )
+            wu_raw = tl.load(
+                wu_ptr + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wu_s0 + (n_start + n_off)[None, :],
+                mask=(k_base + k_off)[:, None] < H,
+            )
+
+            if USE_FP16:
+                acc_g = tl.dot(a_raw.to(tl.float16), wg_raw.to(tl.float16), acc_g)
+                acc_u = tl.dot(a_raw.to(tl.float16), wu_raw.to(tl.float16), acc_u)
+            else:
+                a_f32 = a_raw.to(tl.float32)
+                acc_g = tl.dot(a_f32, wg_raw.to(tl.float32), acc_g)
+                acc_u = tl.dot(a_f32, wu_raw.to(tl.float32), acc_u)
+
+        gate_silu = tl.sigmoid(acc_g) * acc_g
+        result = (gate_silu * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            result,
+            mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < n_tokens,
+        )
+
+for name, use_fp16 in [("fp16_gemm", True), ("fp32_gemm", False)]:
+    out = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    full_kernel[(num_nt,)](
+        x.cuda(), w_gate.cuda(), w_up.cuda(), out,
+        n_tokens, H, I,
+        x.stride(0), w_gate.stride(0), w_up.stride(0), out.stride(0),
+        BLOCK_M=BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N=BLOCK_N, BLOCK_K=BLOCK_K,
+        USE_FP16=use_fp16,
+        num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+    )
+    diff = (out_ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+    print(f"{name}: max_diff={diff.max().item():.6f}  mean={diff.mean().item():.6f}")
+    sign_flips = ((out_ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+    print(f"  sign_flips={sign_flips}/{n_tokens*I}")
args
{
  "filePath": "/home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu/debug_workaround.py",
  "content": "<3060 chars \u2014 see diff>"
}

+"""Test: does Triton load/store bf16 data correctly?"""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+@triton.jit
+def load_store_kernel(in_ptr, out_ptr, N):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    off = pid * 128 + tl.arange(0, 128)
+    mask = off < N
+    x = tl.load(in_ptr + off, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + off, x, mask=mask)
+
+x = torch.randn(1024, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+out = torch.zeros(1024, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+load_store_kernel[(8,)](
+    x.cuda(), out, 1024,
+    num_warps=4,
+)
+print(f"Load/store test: max_diff={(x.cuda() - out).abs().max().item():.6f}")
+
+# Now test: does tl.dot with tiny amounts work?
+@triton.jit
+def tiny_dot(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr,
+             BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a, b)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+# Test with very small values where bf16 has limited precision
+for scale in [0.1, 1.0, 10.0]:
+    a = torch.randn(16, 16, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * scale
+    b = torch.randn(16, 16, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * scale * 0.1
+    ref = a @ b
+    
+    out = torch.zeros(16, 16, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    tiny_dot[(1,)](
+        a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out,
+        BLOCK_M=16, BLOCK_N=16, BLOCK_K=16,
+        num_warps=4,
+    )
+    diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+    sign_flips = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+    print(f"16x16 dot (scale={scale}): max_diff={diff.max().item():.6f} sign_flips={sign_flips}/256")
+    
+# Now test: does the issue happen with any specific row count?
+for M in [1, 2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64]:
+    a = torch.randn(M, 32, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+    b = torch.randn(32, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+    ref = a @ b
+    
+    @triton.jit
+    def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, M, N,
+                    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+        m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+        a = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :], mask=m_off[:, None] < M)
+        b = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * N + n_off[None, :])
+        c = tl.dot(a, b)
+        tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m_off[:, None] < M)
+    
+    out = torch.zeros(M, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+        a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, M, 128,
+        BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+        num_warps=4,
+    )
+    diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+    sign_flips = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+    if sign_flips > 0 or diff.max() > 0.001:
+        print(f"M={M:2d} N=128: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} sign_flips={sign_flips}/{M*128}")
+    else:
+        print(f"M={M:2d} N=128: OK")

+"""Test GEMM at different scales to find where errors start."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, N, a_s0, b_s0, out_s0,
+                BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    n_start = nt * BLOCK_N
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+
+    a = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * a_s0 + k_off[None, :])
+    b = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + (n_start + n_off)[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a, b)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+# Test 1: fixed K=32, N=128, vary M up to 64
+print("Fixed (64,32) x (32,128):")
+a = torch.randn(64, 32, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+b = torch.randn(32, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+ref = a @ b
+out = torch.zeros(64, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+    a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, 128, a.stride(0), b.stride(0), out.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32, num_warps=4,
+)
+diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"  max_diff={diff.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf}")
+
+# Test 2: vary K, keep M,N fixed
+for K in [32, 64, 128, 256, 512, 1024]:
+    a = torch.randn(64, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+    b = torch.randn(K, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+    ref = a @ b
+    
+    @triton.jit
+    def gemm_split(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, a_s0, b_s0, out_s0,
+                   BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+        pid = tl.program_id(0)
+        nt = pid
+        n_start = nt * BLOCK_N
+        m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for k_base in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off2 = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            a2 = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * a_s0 + (k_base + k_off2)[None, :])
+            b2 = tl.load(b_ptr + (k_base + k_off2)[:, None] * b_s0 + (n_start + n_off)[None, :])
+            acc = tl.dot(a2, b2, acc)
+        tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :], acc.to(tl.bfloat16))
+    
+    out = torch.zeros(64, 128, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    gemm_split[(1,)](
+        a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, a.stride(0), b.stride(0), out.stride(0),
+        BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32, num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+    )
+    diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+    sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+    print(f"K={K:4d} ({(K+31)//32} tiles): max_diff={diff.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf}")

+"""Test if stride width in the N dimension causes tl.dot errors."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+M, K = 64, 32
+N_tile = 128
+
+# Case 1: w has shape (32, 128) - contiguous, stride(0)=128
+a = torch.randn(M, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+b1 = torch.randn(K, N_tile, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+ref1 = a @ b1
+
+# Case 2: w has shape (32, 1536) - stride(0)=1536, we access first 128 columns
+w_big = torch.randn(K, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+b2 = w_big[:, :128]  # stride(0) = 1536
+ref2 = a @ b2  # cuBLAS computes the same dot product
+
+print(f"Ref1 vs Ref2 (should be same): max={((ref1-ref2).abs().max().item()):.6f}")
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, b_s0,
+                BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b_t = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, b_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+for name, b, b_s0 in [("stride=128", b1, b1.stride(0)), ("stride=1536", b2, b2.stride(0))]:
+    out = torch.zeros(M, N_tile, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+        a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, b_s0,
+        BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=N_tile, BLOCK_K=K,
+        num_warps=4,
+    )
+    ref = a @ b  # cuBLAS with whatever shape
+    diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+    sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+    print(f"{name}: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf}/{M*N_tile}")
+
+# Test: what if the B tensor has a large stride in the K dimension too?
+# Use a big tensor with K rows but skip rows
+w_wide = torch.randn(4096, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+b3 = w_wide[:K, :N_tile]  # stride(0)=1536, stride(1)=1
+ref3 = a @ b3
+out3 = torch.zeros(M, N_tile, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+    a.cuda(), b3.cuda(), out3, b3.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=N_tile, BLOCK_K=K,
+    num_warps=4,
+)
+diff3 = (ref3.cuda().float() - out3.float()).abs()
+sf3 = ((ref3.cuda() * out3) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"big_view (K=32,N=128 from (4096,1536)): max_diff={diff3.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf3}/{M*N_tile}")
+
+# Test: do sign flips appear with multiple N-tiles?
+out_multi = torch.zeros(M, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+num_nt = triton.cdiv(1536, N_tile)
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_multi(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, b_s0, I,
+               BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    n_start = pid * BLOCK_N
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b_t = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + (n_start + n_off)[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, b_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * I + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+a_big = torch.randn(64, 32, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w_big2 = torch.randn(32, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+ref_big = a_big @ w_big2
+
+gemm_multi[(num_nt,)](
+    a_big.cuda(), w_big2.cuda(), out_multi, w_big2.stride(0), 1536,
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4,
+)
+diff_big = (ref_big.cuda().float() - out_multi.float()).abs()
+sf_big = ((ref_big.cuda() * out_multi) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"\nMulti N-tile (64,32) x (32,1536): max_diff={diff_big.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_big}/{64*1536}")

+"""Test TMA workaround: try small num_stages or different approach."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+M, K, N_tile = 64, 32, 128
+a = torch.randn(M, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w_big = torch.randn(K, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+b = w_big[:, :128]  # stride(0)=1536
+ref = a @ b
+
+print(f"b shape={b.shape}, stride={b.stride()}")
+print(f"cuBLAS ref: mean={ref.float().mean():.6f}")
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, b_s0,
+                BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b_t = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, b_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+# Test with different num_stages
+for ns in [0, 1, 2, 3, 4]:
+    out = torch.zeros(M, N_tile, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    try:
+        gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+            a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, b.stride(0),
+            BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=N_tile, BLOCK_K=K,
+            num_warps=4, num_stages=ns,
+        )
+        diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+        sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+        print(f"num_stages={ns}: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf}/{M*N_tile}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"num_stages={ns}: FAILED - {e}")

assistant
Found root cause: Triton `tl.dot` on SM120 uses TMA for B tensor loading, and TMA produces wrong results when the B stride in K dimension doesn't match the N-tile width. Fix: reorganize weights into tiled layout where each (H, BLOCK_N) sub-block is contiguous.

@@ -0,0 +1,37 @@
+"""Find which strides work and which don't for tl.dot."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+M, K, BN = 64, 32, 128
+a = torch.randn(M, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, b_s0,
+                BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b_t = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, b_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+for stride in [128, 129, 130, 132, 144, 160, 192, 256, 512, 1024, 1536, 2048]:
+    b = torch.randn(K, stride, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+    # We use first BN=128 columns
+    ref = a @ b[:, :BN]
+    out = torch.zeros(M, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    try:
+        gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+            a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, b.stride(0),
+            BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=BN, BLOCK_K=K,
+            num_warps=4,
+        )
+        diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+        sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+        flag = "SIGNFLIP" if sf > 0 else "OK"
+        print(f"stride={stride:4d}: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} {flag} sf={sf}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"stride={stride:4d}: FAILED - {e}")

+"""Test if disabling TMA fixes the stride issue."""
+import os
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+M, K, BN = 64, 32, 128
+a = torch.randn(M, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w_big = torch.randn(K, 1536, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+b = w_big[:, :128]  # view with stride 1536
+ref = a @ b
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_kernel(a_ptr, b_ptr, out_ptr, b_s0,
+                BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    b_t = tl.load(b_ptr + k_off[:, None] * b_s0 + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, b_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_N + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+# Test with TRITON_DISABLE_TMA
+for disable_tma in [None, "1"]:
+    if disable_tma:
+        os.environ["TRITON_DISABLE_TMA"] = "1"
+    else:
+        os.environ.pop("TRITON_DISABLE_TMA", None)
+    
+    out = torch.zeros(M, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    try:
+        gemm_kernel[(1,)](
+            a.cuda(), b.cuda(), out, b.stride(0),
+            BLOCK_M=M, BLOCK_N=BN, BLOCK_K=K,
+            num_warps=4, num_stages=2,
+        )
+        diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+        sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+        flag = "SIGNFLIP" if sf > 0 else "OK"
+        print(f"DISABLE_TMA={disable_tma}: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} {flag} sf={sf}")
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"DISABLE_TMA={disable_tma}: FAILED {e}")

         self.W_up = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(E, H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

+        self._gate_tiled: torch.Tensor | None = None
+        self._up_tiled: torch.Tensor | None = None

+    def _make_tiled(self) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
+        """Reorganize (E, H, I) weights to (E, num_nt, H, BLOCK_N) for TMA-compatible access."""
+        if self._gate_tiled is not None:
+            return self._gate_tiled, self._up_tiled
+        E, H, I = self.E, self.H, self.I
+        bn = 128 if I >= 128 else 32
+        num_nt = I // bn if I % bn == 0 else triton.cdiv(I, bn)
+        pad = num_nt * bn - I
+        if pad > 0:
+            wg = torch.nn.functional.pad(self.W_gate.view(E, H, -1), (0, pad))
+            wu = torch.nn.functional.pad(self.W_up.view(E, H, -1), (0, pad))
+        else:
+            wg = self.W_gate
+            wu = self.W_up
+        gt = wg.view(E, H, num_nt, bn).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+        ut = wu.view(E, H, num_nt, bn).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+        self._gate_tiled = gt
+        self._up_tiled = ut
+        return gt, ut

+"""Verify tiled kernel correctness."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I = 128, 4096, 1536
+E, num_nt = 1, I // 128
+BN = 128
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w_gate = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_up = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+
+# Tiled weights: (E, num_nt, H, BN)
+wg_tiled = w_gate.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+wu_tiled = w_up.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+
+print(f"Tiled shape: {wg_tiled.shape}")
+print(f"Tiled strides: {wg_tiled.stride()}")
+
+# Reference
+gate_ref = x @ w_gate
+up_ref = x @ w_up
+out_ref = torch.nn.functional.silu(gate_ref) * up_ref
+
+@triton.jit
+def tiled_kernel(x_ptr, wg_ptr, wu_ptr, out_ptr, H, I, BN,
+                 x_s0, wg_s0, wg_s1, wg_s2,
+                 wu_s0, wu_s1, wu_s2, out_s0,
+                 BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt_cnt = tl.cdiv(I, BLOCK_N)
+    e = pid // nt_cnt
+    nt = pid % nt_cnt
+    n_start = nt * BLOCK_N
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    n_mask = n_off < I - n_start
+    
+    wg_base = wg_ptr + e * wg_s0 + nt * wg_s1
+    wu_base = wu_ptr + e * wu_s0 + nt * wu_s1
+    
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        m_mask = m_base + m_off < n_tokens
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            k_mask = k_base + k_off < H
+            x_t = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=m_mask[:, None] & k_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            wg_t = tl.load(
+                wg_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wg_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+                mask=k_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            wu_t = tl.load(
+                wu_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wu_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+                mask=k_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            acc_g = tl.dot(x_t, wg_t, acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(x_t, wu_t, acc_u)
+        
+        result = (tl.sigmoid(acc_g) * acc_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            result,
+            mask=m_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+        )
+
+out = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+tiled_kernel[(E * num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), wg_tiled.cuda(), wu_tiled.cuda(), out,
+    n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+    x.stride(0),
+    wg_tiled.stride(0), wg_tiled.stride(1), wg_tiled.stride(2),
+    wu_tiled.stride(0), wu_tiled.stride(1), wu_tiled.stride(2),
+    out.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff = (out_ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+print(f"Tiled kernel vs ref: max_diff={diff.max().item():.6f} mean={diff.mean().item():.6f}")
+sf = ((out_ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"Sign flips: {sf}/{n_tokens*I}")

+"""Verify tiled kernel correctness - all args passed properly."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I, E = 128, 4096, 1536, 1
+BN, num_nt = 128, I // 128
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+wg = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+wu = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+
+wg_t = wg.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+wu_t = wu.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+
+gate_ref = x @ wg
+up_ref = x @ wu
+out_ref = torch.nn.functional.silu(gate_ref) * up_ref
+
+@triton.jit
+def tiled_kernel(
+    x_ptr, wg_ptr, wu_ptr, out_ptr,
+    n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+    x_s0, wg_s0, wg_s1, wg_s2,
+    wu_s0, wu_s1, wu_s2, out_s0,
+    BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt_cnt = tl.cdiv(I, BLOCK_N)
+    e = pid // nt_cnt
+    nt = pid % nt_cnt
+
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    n_mask = n_off < I - nt * BLOCK_N
+
+    wg_base = wg_ptr + e * wg_s0 + nt * wg_s1
+    wu_base = wu_ptr + e * wu_s0 + nt * wu_s1
+
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        m_mask = m_base + m_off < n_tokens
+        acc_g = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        acc_u = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            x_t = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=m_mask[:, None],
+            )
+            wg_t = tl.load(
+                wg_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wg_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+                mask=n_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            wu_t = tl.load(
+                wu_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * wu_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+                mask=n_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            acc_g = tl.dot(x_t, wg_t, acc_g)
+            acc_u = tl.dot(x_t, wu_t, acc_u)
+
+        result = (tl.sigmoid(acc_g) * acc_g * acc_u).to(tl.bfloat16)
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            result,
+            mask=m_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+        )
+
+out = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+tiled_kernel[(E * num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), wg_t.cuda(), wu_t.cuda(), out,
+    n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+    x.stride(0),
+    wg_t.stride(0), wg_t.stride(1), wg_t.stride(2),
+    wu_t.stride(0), wu_t.stride(1), wu_t.stride(2),
+    out.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff = (out_ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+print(f"Tiled kernel: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} mean={diff.mean():.6f}")
+sf = ((out_ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"Sign flips: {sf}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Also test just the GEMM (no silu)
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_only(x_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+              x_s0, w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+              BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    w_base = w_ptr + nt * w_s1
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        m_mask = m_base + m_off < n_tokens
+        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            x_t = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=m_mask[:, None],
+            )
+            w_t = tl.load(
+                w_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+            )
+            acc = tl.dot(x_t, w_t, acc)
+        tl.store(out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+                acc.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=m_mask[:, None])
+
+out_g = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gemm_only[(num_nt,)](x.cuda(), wg_t.cuda(), out_g, n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+    x.stride(0), wg_t.stride(0), wg_t.stride(1), wg_t.stride(2), out_g.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32, num_warps=4, num_stages=3)
+dg = (gate_ref.cuda().float() - out_g.float()).abs()
+sfg = ((gate_ref.cuda() * out_g) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"\nGEMM only (gate): max_diff={dg.max():.6f} sign_flips={sfg}/{n_tokens*I}")

+"""Verify data loading from tiled weights is correct."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+H, I, BN = 4096, 1536, 128
+num_nt = I // BN
+
+# Create data
+w = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_copy = w.clone()
+
+# Tiled version
+w_t = w.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+# Verify: w_t[0, t, :, :] should equal w[:, t*BN:(t+1)*BN]
+for t in range(min(3, num_nt)):
+    print(f"Tile {t}: match={torch.allclose(w_t[0,t,:,:], w[:, t*BN:(t+1)*BN], atol=1e-10)}")
+
+# Now test: does tl.load with tiled pointer give the right data?
+@triton.jit
+def load_test(w_ptr, out_ptr, H, BN,
+              w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+              BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    
+    w_base = w_ptr + nt * w_s1
+    
+    for m_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_M):
+        # Load from tiled weights: shape (H, BN), stride (BN, 1)
+        tile = tl.load(
+            w_base + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+            mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < H,
+        )
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            tile.to(tl.bfloat16),
+            mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < H,
+        )
+
+# Load tile 0 using Triton
+out_t = torch.zeros(H, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+load_test[(1,)](
+    w_t.cuda(), out_t, H, BN,
+    w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out_t.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+ref_tile = w[:, 0:BN]
+diff = (ref_tile.cuda().float() - out_t.float()).abs()
+print(f"\nLoad test tile 0: max_diff={diff.max():.6f}")
+
+# Now test with a K-tile load (BLOCK_K=32, BLOCK_N=128)
+@triton.jit
+def ktile_load(w_ptr, out_ptr, H, BN,
+               w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+               BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    
+    w_base = w_ptr + nt * w_s1
+    
+    for m_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_M):
+        tile = tl.load(
+            w_base + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+            mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < H,
+        )
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            tile.to(tl.bfloat16),
+            mask=(m_base + m_off)[:, None] < H,
+        )
+
+out_k = torch.zeros(H, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+ktile_load[(1,)](
+    w_t.cuda(), out_k, H, BN,
+    w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out_k.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff_k = (ref_tile.cuda().float() - out_k.float()).abs()
+print(f"K-tile load test: max_diff={diff_k.max():.6f}")
+
+# Test: tl.load + tl.dot from tiled weights
+a = torch.randn(64, 32, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+# For K-tile at k=0: B = w[0:32, 0:128]
+ref_gemm = a @ w[:32, :BN]
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_tiled(a_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+               BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    
+    w_base = w_ptr + nt * w_s1
+    
+    a_t = tl.load(a_ptr + m_off[:, None] * BLOCK_K + k_off[None, :])
+    w_t = tl.load(w_base + k_off[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :])
+    c = tl.dot(a_t, w_t)
+    tl.store(out_ptr + m_off[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :], c.to(tl.bfloat16))
+
+out_gemm = torch.zeros(64, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gemm_tiled[(1,)](
+    a.cuda(), w_t.cuda(), out_gemm,
+    w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out_gemm.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4,
+)
+
+diff_g = (ref_gemm.cuda().float() - out_gemm.float()).abs()
+sf_g = ((ref_gemm.cuda() * out_gemm) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"\nGEMM from tiled: max_diff={diff_g.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_g}/{64*BN}")

+"""Test full multi-tile GEMM with tiled weights."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I, E = 128, 4096, 1536, 1
+BN, num_nt = 128, I // 128
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+wg = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+
+# Tiled
+wg_t = wg.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+
+# Reference
+gate_ref = x @ wg
+
+@triton.jit
+def gemm_multi(x_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+               x_s0, w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+               BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt_cnt = tl.cdiv(I, BLOCK_N)
+    e = pid // nt_cnt
+    nt = pid % nt_cnt
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    n_mask = n_off < I - nt * BLOCK_N
+    
+    w_base = w_ptr + e * w_s0 + nt * w_s1
+    
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        m_mask = m_base + m_off < n_tokens
+        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            x_t = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=m_mask[:, None],
+            )
+            w_t = tl.load(
+                w_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+                mask=n_mask[None, :],
+            )
+            acc = tl.dot(x_t, w_t, acc)
+        
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            acc.to(tl.bfloat16),
+            mask=m_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+        )
+
+out = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gemm_multi[(E * num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), wg_t.cuda(), out, n_tokens, H, I, BN,
+    x.stride(0),
+    wg_t.stride(0), wg_t.stride(1), wg_t.stride(2), out.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff = (gate_ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+print(f"Multi-N-tile GEMM: max_diff={diff.max():.6f} mean={diff.mean():.6f}")
+sf = ((gate_ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"Sign flips: {sf}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Per-N-tile breakdown
+for nt in range(num_nt):
+    ns = nt * BN
+    ne = min(ns + BN, I)
+    tile_diff = diff[:, ns:ne]
+    print(f"  NTile {nt} ({ns}:{ne}): max_diff={tile_diff.max():.6f} mean={tile_diff.mean():.6f}")

+"""Debug multi-tile GEMM - pass NUM_NT as constexpr."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I, E, BN = 128, 4096, 1536, 1, 128
+num_nt = I // BN
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_t = w.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+
+ref = x @ w
+
+@triton.jit
+def gm(x_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr, n_tokens, H, I,
+       x_s0, w_s0, w_s1, w_s2, out_s0,
+       BLOCK_M: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
+       NUM_NT: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    e = pid // NUM_NT
+    nt = pid % NUM_NT
+    n_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    n_mask = n_off < I - nt * BLOCK_N
+    
+    w_base = w_ptr + e * w_s0 + nt * w_s1
+    
+    for m_base in range(0, n_tokens, BLOCK_M):
+        m_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_M)
+        m_mask = m_base + m_off < n_tokens
+        acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)
+        
+        for k_base in range(0, H, BLOCK_K):
+            k_off = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+            x_t = tl.load(
+                x_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * x_s0 + (k_base + k_off)[None, :],
+                mask=m_mask[:, None],
+            )
+            w_t = tl.load(
+                w_base + (k_base + k_off)[:, None] * w_s2 + n_off[None, :],
+            )
+            acc = tl.dot(x_t, w_t, acc)
+        
+        tl.store(
+            out_ptr + (m_base + m_off)[:, None] * out_s0 + n_off[None, :],
+            acc.to(tl.bfloat16),
+            mask=m_mask[:, None] & n_mask[None, :],
+        )
+
+out = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gm[(E * num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), w_t.cuda(), out, n_tokens, H, I,
+    x.stride(0), w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out.stride(0),
+    BLOCK_M=64, BLOCK_N=128, BLOCK_K=32,
+    NUM_NT=num_nt,
+    num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff = (ref.cuda().float() - out.float()).abs()
+print(f"Multi-tile (NUM_NT constexpr): max_diff={diff.max():.6f} mean={diff.mean():.6f}")
+sf = ((ref.cuda() * out) < 0).sum().item()
+print(f"Sign flips: {sf}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+for nt in range(num_nt):
+    ns = nt * BN
+    ne = min(ns + BN, I)
+    td = diff[:, ns:ne]
+    print(f"  Tile {nt} ({ns}:{ne}): max={td.max():.6f}")

+"""Compare single-launch multi-tile vs individual single-tile launches."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I, E, BN = 128, 4096, 1536, 1, 128
+num_nt = I // BN
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_t = w.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+ref = x @ w
+
+@triton.jit
+def gm_single(xp, wp, op, N, H, xs, ws2, os0,
+              BM: tl.constexpr, BN2: tl.constexpr, BK: tl.constexpr):
+    mo = tl.arange(0, BM)
+    no = tl.arange(0, BN2)
+    for mb in range(0, N, BM):
+        mm = mb + mo < N
+        ag = tl.zeros((BM, BN2), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for kb in range(0, H, BK):
+            ko = tl.arange(0, BK)
+            ag = tl.dot(tl.load(xp + (mb+mo)[:,None]*xs + (kb+ko)[None,:], mask=mm[:,None]),
+                       tl.load(wp + (kb+ko)[:,None]*ws2 + no[None,:]), ag)
+        tl.store(op + (mb+mo)[:,None]*os0 + no[None,:], ag.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mm[:,None])
+
+# Approach 1: single launch for all tiles
+@triton.jit
+def gm_multi(xp, wp, op, N, H, I, xs, ws0, ws1, ws2, os0,
+             BM: tl.constexpr, BN2: tl.constexpr, BK: tl.constexpr, NNT: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    no = tl.arange(0, BN2)
+    nm = no < I - nt * BN2
+    wb = wp + nt * ws1
+    for mb in range(0, N, BM):
+        mo = tl.arange(0, BM)
+        mm = mb + mo < N
+        ag = tl.zeros((BM, BN2), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for kb in range(0, H, BK):
+            ko = tl.arange(0, BK)
+            ag = tl.dot(tl.load(xp + (mb+mo)[:,None]*xs + (kb+ko)[None,:], mask=mm[:,None]),
+                       tl.load(wb + (kb+ko)[:,None]*ws2 + no[None,:]), ag)
+        tl.store(op + (mb+mo)[:,None]*os0 + no[None,:], ag.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mm[:,None] & nm[None,:])
+
+# Multi-launch: launch each tile separately
+out_separate = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+for nt in range(num_nt):
+    w_slice = w_t[:, nt, :, :].contiguous()
+    temp = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    gm_single[(1,)](
+        x.cuda(), w_slice.cuda(), temp, n_tokens, H,
+        x.stride(0), w_slice.stride(0), temp.stride(0),
+        BM=64, BN2=128, BK=32, num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+    )
+    out_separate[:, nt*BN:(nt+1)*BN] = temp[:, nt*BN:(nt+1)*BN]
+
+diff_sep = (ref.cuda().float() - out_separate.float()).abs()
+sf_sep = ((ref.cuda()*out_separate)<0).sum().item()
+print(f"Separate launches: max_diff={diff_sep.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_sep}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Single launch
+out_single = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gm_multi[(num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), w_t.cuda(), out_single, n_tokens, H, I,
+    x.stride(0), w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out_single.stride(0),
+    BM=64, BN2=128, BK=32, NNT=num_nt, num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff_single = (ref.cuda().float() - out_single.float()).abs()
+sf_single = ((ref.cuda()*out_single)<0).sum().item()
+print(f"Single launch: max_diff={diff_single.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_single}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Compare separate vs single
+diff_ss = (out_separate.cuda().float() - out_single.float()).abs()
+print(f"Separate vs Single: max_diff={diff_ss.max():.6f}")
args
{
  "filePath": "/home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/06_sonic_moe_swiglu/debug_compare.py",
  "content": "<3235 chars \u2014 see diff>"

+"""Compare single-launch multi-tile vs reference, check for consistent errors."""
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+torch.manual_seed(42)
+
+n_tokens, H, I, E, BN = 128, 4096, 1536, 1, 128
+num_nt = I // BN
+
+x = torch.randn(n_tokens, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
+w = torch.randn(H, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.02
+w_t = w.view(1, H, num_nt, BN).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+ref = x @ w
+
+# Approach: directly tile the output using a single-tile kernel per tile
+# Instead of passing temp tensor with I cols, pass one with BN cols per tile
+out_correct = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+for nt in range(num_nt):
+    w_slice = w_t[:, nt, :, :].contiguous().squeeze(0)
+    
+    @triton.jit
+    def gm(xp, wp, op, N, H, xs, ws2, os0,
+           BM: tl.constexpr, BN2: tl.constexpr, BK: tl.constexpr):
+        mo = tl.arange(0, BM)
+        no = tl.arange(0, BN2)
+        for mb in range(0, N, BM):
+            mm = mb + mo < N
+            ag = tl.zeros((BM, BN2), dtype=tl.float32)
+            for kb in range(0, H, BK):
+                ko = tl.arange(0, BK)
+                ag = tl.dot(tl.load(xp + (mb+mo)[:,None]*xs + (kb+ko)[None,:], mask=mm[:,None]),
+                           tl.load(wp + (kb+ko)[:,None]*ws2 + no[None,:]), ag)
+            tl.store(op + (mb+mo)[:,None]*os0 + no[None,:], ag.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mm[:,None])
+    
+    out_nt = torch.zeros(n_tokens, BN, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+    gm[(1,)](
+        x.cuda(), w_slice.unsqueeze(0).cuda(), out_nt, n_tokens, H,
+        x.stride(0), w_slice.stride(0), out_nt.stride(0),
+        BM=64, BN2=128, BK=32, num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+    )
+    out_correct[:, nt*BN:(nt+1)*BN] = out_nt
+
+diff_correct = (ref.cuda().float() - out_correct.float()).abs()
+sf_correct = ((ref.cuda()*out_correct)<0).sum().item()
+print(f"Per-tile contiguous: max_diff={diff_correct.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_correct}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Now try with the multi-tile kernel
+@triton.jit
+def gm_multi(xp, wp, op, N, H, I, xs, ws0, ws1, ws2, os0,
+             BM: tl.constexpr, BN2: tl.constexpr, BK: tl.constexpr, NNT: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    nt = pid
+    no = tl.arange(0, BN2)
+    nm = no < I - nt * BN2
+    wb = wp + nt * ws1
+    for mb in range(0, N, BM):
+        mo = tl.arange(0, BM)
+        mm = mb + mo < N
+        ag = tl.zeros((BM, BN2), dtype=tl.float32)
+        for kb in range(0, H, BK):
+            ko = tl.arange(0, BK)
+            ag = tl.dot(tl.load(xp + (mb+mo)[:,None]*xs + (kb+ko)[None,:], mask=mm[:,None]),
+                       tl.load(wb + (kb+ko)[:,None]*ws2 + no[None,:]), ag)
+        tl.store(op + (mb+mo)[:,None]*os0 + no[None,:], ag.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mm[:,None] & nm[None,:])
+
+out_multi = torch.zeros(n_tokens, I, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')
+gm_multi[(num_nt,)](
+    x.cuda(), w_t.cuda(), out_multi, n_tokens, H, I,
+    x.stride(0), w_t.stride(0), w_t.stride(1), w_t.stride(2), out_multi.stride(0),
+    BM=64, BN2=128, BK=32, NNT=num_nt, num_warps=4, num_stages=3,
+)
+
+diff_multi = (ref.cuda().float() - out_multi.float()).abs()
+sf_multi = ((ref.cuda()*out_multi)<0).sum().item()
+print(f"Multi-tile: max_diff={diff_multi.max():.6f} sign_flips={sf_multi}/{n_tokens*I}")
+
+# Compare correct vs multi
+diff_cm = (out_correct.cuda().float() - out_multi.float()).abs()
+print(f"Correct vs Multi: max_diff={diff_cm.max():.6f}")
